		icon = GFX_decision_TUR_minority_armenia
		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		custom_cost_text = TUR_decision_cost_minority

		available = {
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {

				has_completed_focus = TUR_konstantiniyye_agreement
				has_completed_focus = TUR_return_millet_system
				has_completed_focus = TUR_reform_millet_system
				has_completed_focus = TUR_national_association_program
				has_completed_focus = TUR_enforce_religious_law
				has_completed_focus = TUR_solvetheidentityproblem
			}
			controls_state = 353
			353 = {
				has_state_flag = TUR_armenian_state
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenia_minority }
			}
		}
	    complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
			        has_completed_focus = TUR_anti_imperialism
				}
				add_stability = -0.005
				add_political_power = -15
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
			        has_completed_focus = TUR_national_association_program
				}
				add_stability = 0.005
				add_political_power = -30
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
			        has_completed_focus = TUR_konstantiniyye_agreement
				}
				add_stability = -0.01
				add_war_support = 0.002
				add_political_power = -15
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
			            has_completed_focus = TUR_return_millet_system
						has_completed_focus = TUR_reform_millet_system
					}
				}
				add_stability = -0.01
				add_political_power = -15
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
			            has_completed_focus = TUR_enforce_religious_law
				}
				add_stability = -0.01
				add_political_power = -15
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
			            has_completed_focus = TUR_solvetheidentityproblem
				}
				353 = {
					hidden_effect = {
				        remove_dynamic_modifier = { 
						    modifier = TUR_armenia_minority
					    }
					}
		            add_dynamic_modifier = {
			            modifier = TUR_minority_industry
		            }
					hidden_effect = {
		                add_dynamic_modifier = {
			                modifier = TUR_armenia_minority
		                }
					}
			    }
				add_political_power = -15
			}
			else_if = {
			add_command_power = -15
			353 = {
				add_manpower = -134167
			}
			}
	    }
		remove_effect = {
			353 = {
				clr_state_flag = TUR_armenian_state
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenia_minority }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_solvetheidentityproblem
				}
				353 = {
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_minority_industry }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					353 = {
					    NOT = {
						    is_core_of = TUR
					    }
					}
				}
				353 = {
					add_core_of = TUR
				}
			}
		}

		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		custom_cost_text = TUR_decision_cost_minority
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
					    has_completed_focus = TUR_anti_imperialism
						has_completed_focus = TUR_konstantiniyye_agreement
						has_completed_focus = TUR_reform_millet_system
						has_completed_focus = TUR_return_millet_system
						has_completed_focus = TUR_enforce_religious_law
						has_completed_focus = TUR_solvetheidentityproblem
					}
				}
				has_political_power > 14.99
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_national_association_program
				}
				has_political_power > 29.99
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_enternal_revanchism
				}
				command_power > 14.99
			}
		}

		highlight_states = { state = 453 }

		on_map_mode = map_only

		days_remove = 14

		available = {
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
			    has_completed_focus = TUR_solve_minority_itf
				has_completed_focus = TUR_konstantiniyye_agreement
				has_completed_focus = TUR_return_millet_system
				has_completed_focus = TUR_reform_millet_system
				has_completed_focus = TUR_national_association_program
				has_completed_focus = TUR_enforce_religious_law
				has_completed_focus = TUR_solvetheidentityproblem
			}
			controls_state = 453
			453 = {
				has_state_flag = TUR_arab_state
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
			}
		}
	    complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
			        has_completed_focus = TUR_anti_imperialism
				}
				add_stability = -0.005
				add_political_power = -15
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
			        has_completed_focus = TUR_national_association_program
				}
				add_stability = 0.005
				add_political_power = -30
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
			        has_completed_focus = TUR_konstantiniyye_agreement
				}
				add_stability = -0.01
				add_war_support = 0.002
				add_political_power = -15
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
			            has_completed_focus = TUR_return_millet_system
						has_completed_focus = TUR_reform_millet_system
					}
				}
				add_stability = -0.01
				add_political_power = -15
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
			            has_completed_focus = TUR_enforce_religious_law
				}
				add_stability = 0.005
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
			            has_completed_focus = TUR_solvetheidentityproblem
				}
				453 = {
					hidden_effect = {
				        remove_dynamic_modifier = { 
						    modifier = TUR_arab_minority
					    }
					}
		            add_dynamic_modifier = {
			            modifier = TUR_minority_industry
		            }
					hidden_effect = {
		                add_dynamic_modifier = {
			                modifier = TUR_arab_minority
		                }
					}
			    }
				add_political_power = -15
			}
			else_if = {
			add_command_power = -15
			453 = {
				add_manpower = -4608
			}
			}
	    }
		remove_effect = {
			453 = {
				clr_state_flag = TUR_arab_state
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_solvetheidentityproblem
				}
				453 = {
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_minority_industry }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					453 = {
					    NOT = {
						    is_core_of = TUR
					    }
					}
				}
				453 = {
					add_core_of = TUR
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 4000
				OR = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_anti_imperialism
				has_completed_focus = TUR_konstantiniyye_agreement
				has_completed_focus = TUR_return_millet_system
				has_completed_focus = TUR_reform_millet_system
				has_completed_focus = TUR_national_association_program
				has_completed_focus = TUR_enforce_religious_law
				has_completed_focus = TUR_solvetheidentityproblem
				}
			}
		}
	}

		icon = generic_construction
		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				controls_state = 448
				controls_state = 450
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = naval_base
				province = {
					all_provinces = yes
					limit_to_naval_base = yes
				}
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_open_emergency_ports_built_forts
		}
	}
}

TUR_economy_decision = {
	TUR_british_investment_to_iraq = {
		icon = generic_construction
		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		activation = {
			has_idea = TUR_british_investments_on_iraq
		}
		available = {
		    NOT = {
				has_idea = TUR_british_investments_on_iraq
			}
		}
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 180
		timeout_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_british_already_invested_in_iraq }
					}
					add_resource = {
						type = oil
						amount = 6
						state = 291
					}
					add_resource = {
						type = oil
						amount = 5
						state = 676
					}
					add_resource = {
						type = oil
						amount = 2
						state = 853
					}
					676 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = synthetic_refinery
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = TUR_british_already_invested_in_iraq
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = TUR_british_already_invested_in_iraq
					}
					add_resource = {
						type = oil
						amount = 2
						state = 291
					}
					add_resource = {
						type = oil
						amount = 2
						state = 676
					}
					add_resource = {
						type = oil
						amount = 1
						state = 853

		}
	}

TUR_weapons_import_category = {
	TUR_research_foreign_equipment_production = {
		icon = hol_attract_foreign_investors
		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		available = {
			num_of_civilian_factories > 4
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_6
					has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_5
					has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_4
					has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_3
					has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_2
					has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 10
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 50
		days_re_enable = 50
		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 2
		}
		visible = {
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons
				}
				remove_ideas = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons
					remove_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_2
					remove_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_3
					remove_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_5
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_4
					remove_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_6
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_5
					remove_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_6
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_political_power < 70
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				threat < 0.1
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = TUR_sick_man
					}
					NOT = {
						has_idea = TUR_ODPA
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# early weapon
	TUR_buy_ger_infantry_weapons = {
		icon = generic_industry
		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = FRA
			}
		}
		available = {
			GER = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = ROOT
					value > 0
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_6
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = has_active_purchase_contract
			}
		}
		cost = 10
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 72
		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 3
		}
		visible = {
			GER = {
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			GER = {
				add_offsite_building = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 2
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = {
				flag = has_active_purchase_contract
				days = 60
				value = 1
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			TUR_import_dependence_level_up = yes
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment_0
				amount = 7000
				producer = GER
			}
			GER = {
				add_offsite_building = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = -2
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0.1
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					num_of_civilian_factories < 5
					stockpile_ratio = {
						archetype = infantry_equipment
						ratio > 1
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 10
			}
		}
	}

# ECONOMY
#
economy_decisions = {
	TUR_berlin_baghdad_railway_mission = {
		allowed = {
			original_tag = TUR
		}
		icon = generic_construction
		available = {
			#BREAK MISSION
			has_war_with = GER
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = berlin_baghdad_dispute_ended
						}
						all_controlled_state = {
							OR = {
								state = 341
								state = 347
								state = 49
								state = 348
								state = 344
								state = 350
								state = 352
								state = 676
								state = 291
							}
							free_building_slots = {
								building = infrastructure
								size < 5
								include_locked = yes
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = berlin_baghdad_dispute_ended
						all_controlled_state = {
							OR = {
								state = 341
								state = 347
								state = 49
								state = 348
								state = 344
								state = 350
								state = 352
							}
							free_building_slots = {
								building = infrastructure
								size < 5
								include_locked = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 35
		timeout_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = TUR_berlin_baghdad_railway_state
				}
				clr_state_flag = TUR_berlin_baghdad_railway_state
			}
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = TUR_berlin_baghdad_railway_state
					}
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = TUR_berlin_baghdad_railway_state_blocked
					}
					OR = {
						state = 341
						state = 347
						state = 49
						state = 348
						state = 344
						state = 350
						state = 352
						state = 676
						state = 291
					}
					free_building_slots = {
						building = infrastructure
						size > 5
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_state_flag = TUR_berlin_baghdad_railway_state
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				activate_mission = TUR_berlin_baghdad_railway_mission
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = no
		is_good = yes
	}
	TUR_ger_investments_in_civil_industry = {
		allowed = {
			always = no
		}
		icon = generic_factory
		visible = {
			always = no
			country_exists = GER
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = GER
			}
		}
		cost = 25
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 180
		days_re_enable = 30
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = GER
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			production_speed_industrial_complex_factor = 0.02
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = TUR
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 0
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_war = no
				date < 1913.5.1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				num_of_civilian_factories < 35
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_ger_investments_in_military_industry = {

			has_idea = TUR_sick_man

		remove_effect = {

				limit = {

			}

				add = 10
				num_of_military_factories < 20
			}
		}

			}

				add = 10
				num_of_naval_factories < 20

					has_completed_focus = TUR_order_battleships

				}
			}

propaganda_efforts = {
	TUR_rename_kostantiniyye = {
		allowed = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = TUR
			}
		}
		available = {
			owns_state = 347
			has_full_control_of_state = 347
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = kostantiniyye_is_constantinople
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		cost = 10
		visible = {
			owns_state = 347
			has_full_control_of_state = 347
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = kostantiniyye_is_constantinople
				}
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = no
		complete_effect = {
			set_province_name = {
				id = 9833
				name = CONSTANTINOPLE_PROV
			}
			347 = {
				set_state_name = CONSTANTINOPLE_STATE
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = kostantiniyye_is_constantinople
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_rename_constantinople = {
		allowed = {
			original_tag = TUR
		}
		available = {
			owns_state = 347
			has_full_control_of_state = 347
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_global_flag = kostantiniyye_is_constantinople
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		cost = 10
		visible = {
			owns_state = 347
			has_full_control_of_state = 347
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_global_flag = kostantiniyye_is_constantinople
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = no
		complete_effect = {
			reset_province_name = 9833
			347 = {
				reset_state_name = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_global_flag = kostantiniyye_is_constantinople
			}
		}
	}
}
